# ::::::EATech Note::::::
#
# We have decent number of test cases commented out since we only care about
# a much smaller set than what the Unicode standard covers.
# All tests which have decompositions which result in a mapping of
# 1 character --> 3 or more characters are not supported by EAText and thus
# have been omitted. There are characters which are simply out of our range of supported
# characters so we comment them out here as well.
#
# ::::::End EATech Note::::::
#
# NormalizationTest-6.3.0.txt
# Date: 2012-12-20, 22:18:30 GMT [MD]
#
# Unicode Character Database
# Copyright (c) 1991-2013 Unicode, Inc.
# For terms of use, see http://www.unicode.org/terms_of_use.html
# For documentation, see http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/
#
# Normalization Test Suite
# Format:
#
#   Columns (c1, c2,...) are separated by semicolons
#   They have the following meaning:
#      source; NFC; NFD; NFKC; NFKD
#   Comments are indicated with hash marks
#   Each of the columns may have one or more code points.
#
# CONFORMANCE:
# 1. The following invariants must be true for all conformant implementations
#
#    NFC
#      c2 ==  toNFC(c1) ==  toNFC(c2) ==  toNFC(c3)
#      c4 ==  toNFC(c4) ==  toNFC(c5)
#
#    NFD
#      c3 ==  toNFD(c1) ==  toNFD(c2) ==  toNFD(c3)
#      c5 ==  toNFD(c4) ==  toNFD(c5)
#
#    NFKC
#      c4 == toNFKC(c1) == toNFKC(c2) == toNFKC(c3) == toNFKC(c4) == toNFKC(c5)
#
#    NFKD
#      c5 == toNFKD(c1) == toNFKD(c2) == toNFKD(c3) == toNFKD(c4) == toNFKD(c5)
#
# 2. For every code point X assigned in this version of Unicode that is not specifically
#    listed in Part 1, the following invariants must be true for all conformant
#    implementations:
#
#      X == toNFC(X) == toNFD(X) == toNFKC(X) == toNFKD(X)
#
